Buttons

    *yieldconfirm
        on yield:
            yield 3 lootconfirmtimer
        end
    
    *alwayscrit
        no click
        no text
        class:bigButton
        icon:https://file.garden/XYIlW7cqBDVk_Xim/alwayscrit.png
        tag:alwayscrit
    
	*btrolled
        hidden
        on click:
            $chance1=random(1,256)
            yield 1 bountytablesrolled
            if (($chance1>0) and ($chance1<3))
                yield 1 zrerkring
                yield 1 zrerkringvar
                log <#87e810>On your task you receive: 1x Zrerk's Ring.
                log <b><#e82910>VERY RARE DROP: 1x Zrerk's Ring.
                if (dropcontract=1) yield 61478912 dropcontractrcvd
                if (valuabletokenvar2=1) log <b><#bf08b6>Valuable Drop: [61478912] Coins
                log <b><#441585>RIDICULOUSLY RARE: 1x Zrerk's Ring // 1/256(After rolling Bounty Table, No Item Find Allowed)
                if (ridcontract=1) yield 1 ridcontractrcvd
	        end
            if (($chance1>2) and ($chance1<7))
                yield 1 roanhelmet
                yield 1 roanhelmetvar
                log <#87e810>On your task you receive: 1x Roan Helmet.
                if (dropcontract=1) yield 14944134 dropcontractrcvd

                if (valuabletokenvar2=1) log <b><#bf08b6>Valuable Drop: [14944134] Coins
                log <b><#441585>RIDICULOUSLY RARE: 1x Roan Helmet // 1/64(After rolling Bounty Table, No Item Find Allowed)
                if (ridcontract=1) yield 1 ridcontractrcvd
	        end
            if (($chance1>6) and ($chance1<10))
                yield 1 glavyiorhelmet
                yield 1 glavyiorhelmetvar

                if (valuabletokenvar2=1) log <b><#bf08b6>Valuable Drop: [74222221] Coins

            end

	*ability1
	name:Hard Swing
	desc:[?(greaterhardswingvar1=1)|(Greater Hard Swing) Swing your melee weapon really hard to deal <#6928b8>[94*kyplockpoison]%<#d4d4d4>-<#6928b8>[128*kyplockpoison]%<#d4d4d4> Weapon damage.</>Decreases cooldown of <#56f595>Destruction<#d4d4d4> by 4 and <#56f595>Shadow Leech<#d4d4d4> by 3 seconds.|Swing your melee weapon really hard to deal <#6928b8>[72*kyplockpoison]%<#d4d4d4>-<#6928b8>[110*kyplockpoison]%<#d4d4d4> Weapon damage.]
	on click:if (enemyhp<1) toast You aren't fighting any monsters.
	on click:
	if ((enemyhp>0) and (ability1c=0) and (hp>0) and (bowequipped=0))
	$kypdmgboost=(1+(1-hp/maxhp)*1.71*kypseteffect)
	yield -(ability8at) ability8at
	$extroll=random(1,(10000*(1-alwayscritvar)+(alwayscritvar)))
	if (($extroll)>=(critchance*100))
	hide ability1
	yield 12 ability1c
	if (zarkossword2=1 or nyzarkossword2=1) yield 1 ability1c
	if ((elderdragonsword2=1) and (ability3at=0)) yield -2 ability3c
	yield (floor(random((attackmin*(0.72+greaterhardswingvar1*0.22)*atkmulti*ability8stackeddmg*(daggerdmg*daggerequipped+1)*(eplisordamage+1)*(kypcursedmgr)*(kyplockpoison)*(1-(kypcorruptionstack/100))*(1+kypragestack/100)*(1+shatterdmgred/100)*$kypdmgboost*(1+kypcapespecvar*0.25)),(attackmax*(1.10+greaterhardswingvar1*0.18)*atkmulti*ability8stackeddmg*(daggerdmg*daggerequipped+1)*(eplisordamage+1)*(kypcursedmgr)*(kyplockpoison)*(1-(kypcorruptionstack*1.5/100))*(1+kypragestack/100)*(1+shatterdmgred/100)*$kypdmgboost*(1+kypcapespecvar*0.25))))) atk2
	if (greaterhardswingvar1=1)
	yield -4 ability8c
	yield -3 ability6c
	end
	yield -(ability8stackeddmg-1) ability8stackeddmg
	do larphroll with larphroll
	yield (floor(atk2*dmgpvar3)) atk2
	if (zarkossword2=1 or nyzarkossword2=1) yield (atk2*0.25) atk2
	if (hp<maxhp/4) yield (floor(atk2*ragevar3)) atk2
	if (kypcursevar=1)
	if (dmgtextdyeequipped=0) log You swing hard and heal Kyplonzin with <#98fc03>[atk2]<#000000> HP!
	if (yellowdyetoggle=1) log You swing hard and heal Kyplonzin with <#dbd630>[atk2]<#000000> HP!
	do crush with statchances
	do shatter with statchances
	do bleed with statchances
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypcursevar=1)) log Flawless run failed!(Curses/Hard Swing Heal)</#>
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypcursevar=1)) yield 1 kypflawfailed
	else
	if (dmgtextdyeequipped=0) log You swing hard and deal <#98fc03>[atk2]<#000000> damage! 
	if (yellowdyetoggle=1) log You swing hard and deal <#dbd630>[atk2]<#000000> damage!
	do crush with statchances
	do shatter with statchances
	do bleed with statchances
	end
	if (kypcursevar=4)
	yield -ceil(atk2/10) hp
	log -<#b52218>[(ceil(atk2/10))]<#000000> HP(Reflect)
	end	
	if (dungmonstype=3)
	yield -ceil(atk2/20) hp
	log -<#b52218>[(ceil(atk2/20))]<#000000> HP(Shell Reflect)
	end	
	if (kypcursevar=6)
	$rand=random(5,12)
	yield ($rand/100) kypcursedmg
	end
	if (iceshatter2=1) yield 0.03 iceshatterdmg
	if (kypsoulactive=1) yield -(atk2) kypsoulhp
	if (kypmanashieldactive=1) yield -(atk2) kypmanashieldhp
	if ((kyprefbombactive=1) and (kyprefbombstimer2=2))
	if (kyprefbombsill2=1)
	yield -1500 hp
	log -<#b52218>1500<#000000> HP(Reflex Bombs)
	log You attack an illusion bomb and receive massive damage!
	$rand=random(1,3)
	if ($rand=1) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Bravo.
	if ($rand=2) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Are you blind?
	if ($rand=3) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Wake up...
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) log Flawless run failed!(Reflex Bombs/Illusion Bomb Attacked)</#>
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) yield 1 kypflawfailed
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer) kyprefbombstimer
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer2) kyprefbombstimer2
	yield -1 kyprefbombsleft
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill2
	else
	yield -150 hp
	log -<#b52218>150<#000000> HP(Reflex Bombs)
	log You reflect the bomb and reduce the damage received!
	$rand=random(1,3)
	if ($rand=1) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Decent.
	if ($rand=2) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Not bad.
	if ($rand=3) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Alright.
	if (kyplonzinphase=4) yield -2 kypcorruptionstack
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer) kyprefbombstimer
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer2) kyprefbombstimer2
	yield -1 kyprefbombsleft
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill2
	end
	end
	yield -(eplisordamage) eplisordamage
	if (hardswingcontract=1) yield (atk2) hardswingcdamagedone
	if ((ability3at>0) and (empowercontract=1)) yield (atk2*(atkmulti-1)) empowercdamagedone
	if (skybreaker2=1 or nyskybreaker2=1) yield ceil(atk2/7) otdamagevar
	if ((amadineboots2=1) and (amadineleggings2=1) and (amadinechestplate2=1) and (amadinehelmet2=1) and (chance(10%)) and (svar5=0))
	yield 1 svar5
	end
	if (svar5>0)
	yield -(atk2/5) enemyhp
	log Amadine armor set hit <#98fc03>[atk2/5]<#000000> damage! <#98fc03>([atk2/5+atk2])
	yield -1 svar5
	end
	if (drscshieldvar1=1)
	yield (atk2*3) drscshieldvar2
	end
	if (drscillusionvar1=1)
	yield -(atk2+floor(((drscenragevar*floor(attackmax/attackmin))*ffssoul2))) drscillusionvar2
	end
	if (chance(5%)) do click with reheerdamage
	if (krymsword2=1)
	yield ceil(atk2/13) hp2
	log +<#45ff17>[hp2]<#000000> HP(Leech)
	yield (hp2) hp
	yield -(hp2) hp2
	end
	if (soulnecklace2=1)
	yield ceil(atk2/15) hp2
	log +<#45ff17>[hp2]<#000000> HP(Soul Necklace)
	yield (hp2) hp
	yield -(hp2) hp2
	end
	if (ffssoul2=1)
	yield ceil(atk2/15) hp2
	log +<#45ff17>[hp2]<#000000> HP(FF's Soul)
	yield (hp2) hp
	yield -(hp2) hp2
	end
	if ((ffssoul2=1) and (luthritecape2=1) and (chance(2%)))
	yield -3000 enemyhp
	log A <#602080>Luthrite Star<#000000> falls from the sky and hits the enemy for <#98fc03>3000!
	if (drscillusionvar1=1)
	yield -4500 drscillusionvar2
	log -<#b52218>4500<#000000> Prane HP(Luthrite Star)
	end
	end
	if (kypcursevar=1)
	yield (atk2) enemyhp
	else
	yield -(atk2) enemyhp
	end
	if (drscrevivalvar=1)
	if (drscillusionvar1=1)
	yield -(atk2/1.5+floor(((drscenragevar*floor(attackmax/attackmin))*ffssoul2))) drscillusionvar2
	end
	yield -(atk2/1.5) enemyhp
	log <b>You dealt <#7221b0>[atk2/1.5]<#000000> extra damage to Drasconix!
	end
	yield (atk2*1.5*magisvar3) attackxp
	if ((zombietask=1) and (fightzombie=1) and (zombiecurrentkills<zombiereqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	if ((azombietask=1) and (fightazombie=1) and (azombiecurrentkills<azombiereqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	if ((demontask=1) and (fightdemon=1) and (demoncurrentkills<demonreqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	if ((dinosaurtask=1) and (fightdinosaur=1) and (dinosaurcurrentkills<dinosaurreqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	if ((zrerktask=1) and (fightkzombie=1) and (zrerkcurrentkills<zrerkreqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	if ((krysmtask=1) and (fightkrysm=1) and (krysmcurrentkills<krysmreqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	if ((drsctask=1) and (fightdrasconix=1) and (drsccurrentkills<drscreqkills)) yield (atk2*0.5*magisvar3) bountyxp
	yield -(atk2) atk2
	if (attackxp>attackxpreq)
	yield (attackxpreq*1.135-attackxpreq) attackxpreq
	yield 1 attacklevel
	toast You leveled up to level [attacklevel]!
	if ((attacklevel=5) and (rollnumber=1))
	log You unlocked <b>Armored Zombie</b> assignment for Bounty Hunter!
	yield 1 rollnumber
	end
	if ((attacklevel=15) and (rollnumber=2))
	log You unlocked <b>Demon</b> assignment for Bounty Hunter!
	yield 1 rollnumber
	end
	if ((attacklevel=30) and (rollnumber=3))
	log You unlocked <b>Dinosaur</b> assignment for Bounty Hunter!
	yield 1 rollnumber
	end
	if ((attacklevel=50) and (rollnumber=4))
	log You unlocked <b>Zrerk</b> assignment for Bounty Hunter!
	yield 1 rollnumber
	end
	if ((attacklevel=65) and (rollnumber=5))
	log You unlocked <b>Krysm</b> assignment for Bounty Hunter!
	yield 1 rollnumber
	end
	if ((attacklevel=80) and (rollnumber=6))
	log You unlocked <b>Drasconix</b> assignment for Bounty Hunter!
	yield 1 rollnumber
	end
	end
	if (bountyxp>bountyxpreq)
	yield (bountyxpreq*1.137-bountyxpreq) bountyxpreq
	yield 1 bountylevel
	toast Your bounty level is now [bountylevel]!
	end
	end
	if (($extroll)<(critchance*100) and ($extroll)>0)
	hide ability1
	yield 12 ability1c
	if (zarkossword2=1 or nyzarkossword2=1) yield 3 ability1c
	if ((elderdragonsword2=1) and (ability3at=0)) yield -2 ability3c
	yield (floor(random((attackmin*(1.44+greaterhardswingvar1*0.44)*atkmulti*(daggerdmg*daggerequipped+1)*ability8stackeddmg*(eplisordamage+1)*(kypcursedmgr)*(kyplockpoison)*(1-(kypcorruptionstack/100))*(1+kypragestack/100)*(1+shatterdmgred/100)*$kypdmgboost*(1+kypcapespecvar*0.25)),(attackmax*(2.20+greaterhardswingvar1*0.36)*atkmulti*ability8stackeddmg*(eplisordamage+1)*(kypcursedmgr)*(kyplockpoison)*(1-(kypcorruptionstack*1.5/100))*(1+kypragestack/100)*(1+shatterdmgred/100)*$kypdmgboost*(1+kypcapespecvar*0.25))))) atk2
	if (greaterhardswingvar1=1)
	yield -4 ability8c
	yield -3 ability6c
	end
	yield -(ability8stackeddmg-1) ability8stackeddmg
	do larphroll with larphroll
	yield (floor(atk2*dmgpvar3)) atk2
	if (zarkossword2=1 or nyzarkossword2=1) yield (atk2*0.25) atk2
	if (hp<maxhp/4) yield (floor(atk2*ragevar3)) atk2
	if (kypcursevar=1)
	if (crittextdyeequipped=0) log You swing hard and heal Kyplonzin with <#d925c7>[atk2]<#000000> HP!
	if (reddyetoggle=1) log You swing hard and heal Kyplonzin with <#f54545>[atk2]<#000000> HP!
	if (bluedyetoggle=1) log You swing hard and heal Kyplonzin with <#0a32c2>[atk2]<#000000> HP!
	do crush with statchances
	do shatter with statchances
	do bleed with statchances
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypcursevar=1)) log Flawless run failed!(Curses/Hard Swing Heal)</#>
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypcursevar=1)) yield 1 kypflawfailed
	else
	if (crittextdyeequipped=0) log You swing hard and deal <#d925c7>[atk2]<#000000> damage!
	if (reddyetoggle=1) log You swing hard and deal <#f54545>[atk2]<#000000> damage!
	if (bluedyetoggle=1) log You swing hard and deal <#0a32c2>[atk2]<#000000> damage!
	do crush with statchances
	do shatter with statchances
	do bleed with statchances
	end
	if (kypseteffect=1)
	yield (bleedingdmg/4) bleedingdmg
	yield (shatterdmgred/4) shatterdmgred
	yield (crushdmgred/4) crushdmgred
	end
	if (kyplonzinphase=4) yield -2 kypcorruptionstack
	if (kypcritrushactive=1)
	yield -1 kypcritrushleft
	end
	if (kypcursevar=4)
	yield -ceil(atk2/10) hp
	log -<#b52218>[(ceil(atk2/10))]<#000000> HP(Reflect)
	end
	if (dungmonstype=3)
	yield -ceil(atk2/20) hp
	log -<#b52218>[(ceil(atk2/20))]<#000000> HP(Shell Reflect)
	end	
	if (kypcursevar=6)
	$rand=random(5,12)
	yield ($rand/100) kypcursedmg
	end
	if (kypsoulactive=1) yield -(atk2) kypsoulhp
	if (kypmanashieldactive=1) yield -(atk2) kypmanashieldhp
	if ((kyprefbombactive=1) and (kyprefbombstimer2=2))
	if (kyprefbombsill2=1)
	yield -1500 hp
	log -<#b52218>1500<#000000> HP(Reflex Bombs)
	log You attack an illusion bomb and receive massive damage!
	$rand=random(1,3)
	if ($rand=1) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Bravo.
	if ($rand=2) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Are you blind?
	if ($rand=3) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Wake up...
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) log Flawless run failed!(Reflex Bombs/Illusion Bomb Attacked)</#>
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) yield 1 kypflawfailed
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer) kyprefbombstimer
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer2) kyprefbombstimer2
	yield -1 kyprefbombsleft
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill2
	else
	yield -150 hp
	log -<#b52218>150<#000000> HP(Reflex Bombs)
	log You reflect the bomb and reduce the damage received!
	$rand=random(1,3)
	if ($rand=1) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Decent.
	if ($rand=2) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Not bad.
	if ($rand=3) log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Alright.
	if (kyplonzinphase=4) yield -2 kypcorruptionstack
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer) kyprefbombstimer
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer2) kyprefbombstimer2
	yield -1 kyprefbombsleft
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill
	yield -1 kyprefbombsill2
	end
	end
	yield 0.03 iceshatterdmg
	if (eplisorring2=1) do click with extrahit

	if ((larphersword2=1) and (azombietask=1) and (fightazombie=1) and (azombiecurrentkills<azombiereqkills)) yield (round(atk*0.32)) atk
	if ((larphersword2=1) and (demontask=1) and (fightdemon=1) and (demoncurrentkills<demonreqkills)) yield (round(atk*0.32)) atk

	*miningiron
	on click:
	$accroll=random(1,10000)
	if (($accroll<(10000-((floor((orehard*2000)/(miningprecision)))))) and (miningprecision>0) and (miningpower>0))
	$damageroll=ceil((random(ceil(miningpower*0.5/(orehard/2.5)),(ceil(miningpower*1.5/(orehard/2.5)))))*(minersoutfitb))

	log You hit and deal <#47fffc>[$damageroll]<#000000> damage to the ore.
	$randomroll=random(1,512-ceil((itemfind+30*spelunkerring2)/30))
	$randomroll2=random(1,2048-ceil((itemfind+30*spelunkerring2)/20))

	log <b><#39fad3>A spirit appears floating around you.
	spawn spirit
	end
	if (($randomroll2=1) and (luthritecape2=1))
	log  <b><#992e91>A Luthrite Star appears!
	spawn luthritestar
	end
	if (orehp=0)
	yield -(orevenomleft) orevenomleft
	yield -(orevenomtick) orevenomtick
	yield 33 miningxp
	if (miningxp>miningxpreq)
	yield (miningxpreq*1.15-miningxpreq) miningxpreq
	yield 1 mininglevel
	toast You leveled up to mining level [mininglevel]!
	do click with hidenfromview
	end
	$ironbarroll=random(1,(ceil(miningprecision/(orehard))))
	$steelchance=random(1,(ceil((orehard*20)/miningprecision)))
	$steelbarroll=random(1,(ceil(miningprecision/(orehard*5))))
	$ringroll=random(1,(ceil(1666000/((itemfind+30*spelunkerring2)/10+1))))
	yield ($ironbarroll) ironbarvar
	yield ($ironbarroll) ironbar
	log You received [$ironbarroll]x Iron Bars.
	if (ironcontract=1) yield 1 ironcontractmined
	yield (maxorehp) orehp
	if ($steelchance=1)
	log You received [$steelbarroll]x Steel Bars.
	yield ($steelbarroll) steelbarvar
	yield ($steelbarroll) steelbar
	end

	yield 1 spelunkerring
	yield 1 spelunkerringvar
	log <b>You find a Spelunker Ring

	if (valuabletokenvar2=1) log <b><#bf08b6>Valuable Drop: [14877777] Coins
	end
	end
	end
	if (($accroll>(10000-((floor((orehard*2000)/(miningprecision))))-1)) and (miningprecision>0) and (miningpower>0))
	log You miss and don't do damage to the ore. ([min((floor(((orehard*2000)/(miningprecision))/100)), 100)].[100*((((orehard*2000)/(miningprecision))/100)-(((floor(((orehard*2000)/(miningprecision))/100)))))]% Chance to miss)
	end
	end

	*blackholebutton

	*snowtokenpricechange
	on click:
	$value=random((30000-ceil(snowcriticalprice/6000)),(500000-ceil(snowcriticalprice/600)))
	if (snowcriticalprice>300000000) 
	$value=(($value-200000)*5)
	end
	yield $value snowcriticalprice
	end
	
	*dyepricechanger
	on redchange:
	$reddyeprice2c=random(1,96)
	$reddyeprice3c=random(1,96)
	if ((reddyeprice2>200) and ($reddyeprice2c=1))
	yield -random(40,160) reddyeprice2
	end
	if ((reddyeprice2<800) and ($reddyeprice2c=2))
	yield random(40,160) reddyeprice2
	end
	if ((reddyeprice3>10000000) and ($reddyeprice3c=1))
	yield -random(1000000,6000000) reddyeprice3
	end
	if ((reddyeprice3<40000000) and ($reddyeprice3c=2))
	yield random(1000000,6000000) reddyeprice3
	end
	$value=random((-(ceil(reddyeprice/reddyeprice2))),(reddyeprice3-ceil(reddyeprice/100)))
	$pricechangeran=random(1,32)
	if ($pricechangeran=1)
	$value=$value+random(40000000,70000000)
	end
	if ($pricechangeran=2)
	$value=$value-random(30000000,50000000)
	end
	yield $value reddyeprice
	end
	on bluechange:
	$bluedyeprice2c=random(1,96)
	$bluedyeprice3c=random(1,96)
	if ((bluedyeprice2>250) and ($bluedyeprice2c=1))
	yield -random(60,200) bluedyeprice2
	end
	if ((bluedyeprice2<850) and ($bluedyeprice2c=2))
	yield random(60,200) bluedyeprice2
	end
	if ((bluedyeprice3>2000000) and ($bluedyeprice3c=1))
	yield -random(400000,1600000) bluedyeprice3
	end
	if ((bluedyeprice3<13000000) and ($bluedyeprice3c=2))
	yield random(400000,1600000) bluedyeprice3
	end
	$value=random((-(ceil(bluedyeprice/bluedyeprice2))),(bluedyeprice3-ceil(bluedyeprice/100)))
	$pricechangeran=random(1,32)
	if ($pricechangeran=1)
	$value=$value+random(10000000,25000000)
	end
	if ($pricechangeran=2)
	$value=$value-random(6000000,16000000)
	end
	yield $value bluedyeprice
	end
	on yellowchange:
	$yellowdyeprice2c=random(1,96)
	$yellowdyeprice3c=random(1,96)
	if ((yellowdyeprice2>200) and ($yellowdyeprice2c=1))
	yield -random(40,160) yellowdyeprice2
	end
	if ((yellowdyeprice2<800) and ($yellowdyeprice2c=2))
	yield random(40,160) yellowdyeprice2
	end
	if ((yellowdyeprice3>20000000) and ($yellowdyeprice3c=1))
	yield -random(4000000,16000000) yellowdyeprice3
	end
	if ((yellowdyeprice3<100000000) and ($yellowdyeprice3c=2))
	yield random(4000000,16000000) yellowdyeprice3
	end
	$value=random((-(ceil(yellowdyeprice/yellowdyeprice2))),(yellowdyeprice3-ceil(yellowdyeprice/100)))
	$pricechangeran=random(1,32)
	if ($pricechangeran=1)
	$value=$value+random(70000000,120000000)
	end
	if ($pricechangeran=2)
	$value=$value-random(50000000,85000000)
	end
	yield $value yellowdyeprice
	end
	
	
	*pranehealing
	on praneheal:
	if ((drscillusionvar1=1) and (drscillusionvar2>0) and (enemyhp>0) and (fightdrasconix=1))
	yield ceil(100+(drscenragevar/5)) enemyhp
	log +<#19d604>[ceil(100+(drscenragevar/5))] Enemy HP (Prane's Healing)
	if (enemyhp>enemymaxhp) log <#25bab3><b>OVERHEALING!
	yield -(ticker3) ticker3
	end
	end

	yield -(kypcritrushtimer) kypcritrushtimer
	yield -1 kypspecactive
	yield -(kyptimer) kyptimer
	end
	if ((kypcritrushtimer=0) and (kypcritrushactive=1))
	if (kyplonzinphase>2)
	log -<#b52218>[(1500*kypcritrushleft)]<#000000> HP(Crit Rush)</#>
	yield -(1500*kypcritrushleft) hp
	else
	log -<#b52218>[(1200*kypcritrushleft)]<#000000> HP(Crit Rush)</#>
	yield -(1200*kypcritrushleft) hp
	end
	log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Can't crit, can't kill.
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) log Flawless run failed!(Crit Rush/Crits Left)</#>
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) yield 1 kypflawfailed
	yield -1 kypcritrushactive
	yield -1 kypspecactive
	yield -(kypcritrushleft) kypcritrushleft
	yield -(kyptimer) kyptimer
	end
	end

//Soul Vacuum Special
	*kypsoulactive
	always hidden
	*kypsouldamage
	on earn:
	if ((kypsouldamage>250) and (kypsoulactive=1))
	if ((kypflawfailed=0) and (kypspecactive=1)) log Flawless run failed!(Soul Leech/Low DMG)</#>

	yield -1 kypspecactive
	yield -1 kypsoulactive
	yield -(kypsouldamage) kypsouldamage
	yield -(kypsoulhp) kypsoulhp
	log <#380810>Kyplonzin:<#000000>Your soul is now MINE!
	end
	end
	always hidden

	yield -1 kypspecactive
	yield -1 kypsoulactive
	yield -(kypsouldamage) kypsouldamage

	end

	*dialog1
	always hidden
	on earn:
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#fc3003> Blood Crystal<#000000>... BLEED DEEPLY!
	log You start to lose health very quickly!
	yield 1 drscbcvar1
	yield -1 dialog1
	end

	*dialog2
	always hidden
	on earn:
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#642c94> Shadow Crystal<#000000>... SHIELD ME!
	yield 1 drscscvar1
	yield -1 dialog2
	end

	*dialog3
	always hidden
	on earn:
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#52ba25> Nature Crystal<#000000>... PRANE, AID ME!
	log Deal [ceil(750+(drscenragevar*5))] Damage to Drasconix to kill Prane!
	yield 1 drscncvar1
	yield -1 dialog3
	end

	*dialog4
	always hidden
	on earn:
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#56c770> I WON'T DIE <#7eff5e><b>YET!
	yield -1 dialog4
	end

	*dialog5
	always hidden
	on earn:
	$roll=random(1,5)
	if ($roll=1)
	log <#8bd16f>Drasconix:<#000000> NO!
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#000000> SUCH A FAILURE.
	end
	if ($roll=2)
	log <#8bd16f>Drasconix:<#000000> Don't leave me...
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#000000> PATHETIC.
	end
	if ($roll=3)
	log <#8bd16f>Drasconix:<#000000> The corruption is too strong!
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#000000> HAHAHAHA!
	end
	if ($roll=4)
	log <#8bd16f>Drasconix:<#000000> Try harder!
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#000000> WHAT A FOOL.
	end
	if ($roll=5)
	log <#8bd16f>Drasconix:<#000000> He's too powerful!
	log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#000000> WEAK.
	end
	log Ended Enrage at: [drscenragevar]%
	log Ended Killstreak at: [drscenragecurrent]
	yield -(drscenragevar) drscenragevar
	yield -(drscenragecurrent) drscenragecurrent
	yield -1 dialog5 
	end

	*dialog6
	always hidden
	on earn:
		log <#3d5932>Corrupted Drasconix:<#000000>Finally...
		log <#8bd16f>Drasconix:<#000000>Thank you.
	yield -1 dialog6 
	end

	*hp
		text:HP [ceil(hp)] / [(floor(maxhp*(1-kypcorruptionstack/100)))]
		name:HP
		desc:Your current HP, don't let it go down to 0 or you get a game over(lose coins).[?(darkerousstacks>0)|<.><#344cfa>Darkerous Liquid Stacks: [darkerousstacks]</#>]
		start with:100
		on earn:if (hp>=(maxhp*(1-kypcorruptionstack/100))) yield -(hp-maxhp*(1-kypcorruptionstack/100)) hp
	tag:playerhp
	on lose:
	if (hp<1)
	if (drsclosebattle=1)
	yield -1 drscachvar1
	yield -(ticker3) ticker3
	yield -(ticker2) ticker2
	yield -(kypdialogtimer) kypdialogtimer
	yield -(kypdialogvar) kypdialogvar
	yield -(drasconixvar1) drasconixvar1
	yield -(drasconixvar2) drasconixvar2
	yield -(drscbleedvar1) drscbleedvar1
	yield -(drscbleedticker1) drscbleedticker1
	yield -(drscshieldvar1) drscshieldvar1
	yield -(drscshieldvar2) drscshieldvar2
	yield -(drscshieldticker1) drscshieldticker1
	yield -(drscillusionvar1) drscillusionvar1
	yield -(drscillusionvar2) drscillusionvar2
	yield -1 drscrevivalvar
	yield 1 dialog5
	end
	if (fightkyplonzin=1)
	yield -4 kyplonzinphase
	yield -1 kyprefbombactive
	yield -(kyptimer) kyptimer
	yield -(kypp3damage) kypp3damage
	yield 1 kypp3damage
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer) kyprefbombstimer
	yield -(kyprefbombsill) kyprefbombsill
	yield -(kyprefbombsill2) kyprefbombsill2
	yield -(kyprefbombstimer2) kyprefbombstimer2
	yield -(kypflawfailed) kypflawfailed
	yield -(kypsoulactive) kypsoulactive
	yield -(kypspecactive) kypspecactive
	yield -(kypsouldamage) kypsouldamage
	yield -(kypsoulhp) kypsoulhp
	yield -(kypmanashieldactive) kypmanashieldactive
	yield -(kypmanashieldhp) kypmanashieldhp
	yield -(kypmanashieldtimer) kypmanashieldtimer
	yield -(kypcursevar) kypcursevar
	yield -(kypcursedmg) kypcursedmg
	yield 1 kypcursedmg
	yield -(kypcursedmgr) kypcursedmgr
	yield 1 kypcursedmgr
	yield -(kypbinddmg) kypbinddmg
	yield 1 kypbinddmg
	yield -(kypruptiondmg) kypruptiondmg
	yield -(kypextradmg) kypextradmg
	yield -(kypcritrushactive) kypcritrushactive
	yield -(kypcritrushleft) kypcritrushleft
	yield -(kypcritrushtimer) kypcritrushtimer
	yield 1 kypextradmg
	yield -(kyplockactive) kyplockactive
	yield -(kyplockcharge) kyplockcharge
	yield -(kyplockpoison) kyplockpoison
	yield 1 kyplockpoison
	yield -(kypp3damage) kypp3damage
	yield 1 kypp3damage
	yield -(kypp3poisonstack) kypp3poisonstack
	yield -(kypp3poisonstacktime) kypp3poisonstacktime
	yield -(kypcorruptionstack) kypcorruptionstack
	yield -(kypragestack) kypragestack
	yield -(kypsiphonactive) kypsiphonactive
	yield -(kypsiphonsiphoned) kypsiphonsiphoned
	yield -(kypcorrbombactive) kypcorrbombactive
	yield -(kypcorrbombpopped) kypcorrbombpopped
	yield -(kypcorrbombtimer) kypcorrbombtimer
	yield -(kypcorrbombspawned) kypcorrbombspawned
	yield -(kypp4dialog) kypp4dialog
	end
	if (enterdungeon1=1)
	hide contdung
	hide lootdung
	hide receivedung1loot
	hide receivedung2loot
	hide receivedung3loot
	do died with dungwaveclear
	end
	if (enterdungeon2=1)
	hide contdung
	hide lootdung
	hide receivedung1loot
	hide receivedung2loot
	hide receivedung3loot
	do died with dungwaveclear
	end
	if (enterdungeon3=1)
	hide contdung
	hide lootdung
	hide receivedung1loot
	hide receivedung2loot
	hide receivedung3loot
	do died with dungwaveclear
	end
	do endbattleloss with endbattlelose
	end
	end

	*lootzombie
	text:Loot Zombie
	name:Loot Zombie
	desc:Click this button to loot the zombie you just killed, and start to regenerate hp.
	limit:1
	start with:1
	no buy
	on click:lose 1 zmblosebattle
	on click:lose 1 zmbvictorybattle
	on click:
	yield -1 attackplayer
	show tag:enemy
	show shopentrance
	if (zmbkc=5)
	yield 1 woodendagger
	yield 1 woodendaggervar
	yield 1 woodendaggervar2
	if (dropcontract=1) yield 21 dropcontractrcvd
	log <#eda366>First time bonus!
	end
	yield (random(2,20)) coins2
	log Zombie dropped <#ebe834>[floor(coins2*coinpvar3)] coins<#000000>
	yield floor(coins2*coinpvar3) coins
	yield -(coins2) coins2
	yield -1 bregenhp
	if (bregenhp=0) yield 1 regenhp
	yield 1 zmbkc
	hide lootzombie
	show minebutton1
	if ((zombietask=0) and (azombietask=0) and (demontask=0) and (dinosaurtask=0) and (zrerktask=0) and (krysmtask=0) and (drsctask=0)) show bountyhunter
	if ((zombietask=1) and (zombiecurrentkills<zombiereqkills))
	if (zombiecurrentkills<zombiereqkills) yield 1 zombiecurrentkills
	$frontersroll=round(random(1,2048/(bountylevel/3)))
	if ($frontersroll=1)
	yield 1 frontershield
	yield 1 frontershieldvar
	yield 1 frontershieldvar2
	if (dropcontract=1) yield 6412 dropcontractrcvd
	log <b><#1f41db>RARE DROP: 1x Fronter Shield // 1/[round(2048/(bountylevel/3))](No Item Find Allowed, only on Zombie Bounty task)
	end
	yield 15 bountyxp
	log +15 Bounty XP
	$raretable=round(random(1,(1024/(bountylevel/30))))
	if ($raretable=1)
	do click with btrolled
	end
	end
	yield (random(1,10)) chance1
	$random1=random(1,400)
	$random2=random(1,(rdtchance-rdroppervar1))
	$random3=random(1,128)
	$random4=random(1,40)
	yield -1 attackplayer
	yield -1 attackenemy
	if ($random1=1)
	yield 1 regencodexvar
	yield 1 regencodex
	log <b><#fffc40>The monster dropped a strange looking codex: You received 1x Regeneration Ability Codex.
	log <b><#1f41db>RARE DROP: 1x Regeneration Ability Codex // 1/400(No Item Find Allowed)
	if (dropcontract=1) yield 2134 dropcontractrcvd
	end
	if ($random2=1)
	yield 1 rdtrolled
	$roll=random(1,4096)
	if (($roll<112) and ($roll>0))
	yield 25000 coins
	log <#f7a736>The monster shines and disappears leaving some coins behind, you received: 25000x Coins
	end
	if (($roll<304) and ($roll>111))
	yield 2 mediumcasketvar
	yield 2 mediumcasket
	log <#f7a736>The monster shines and disappears leaving items behind, you received: 2x Casket (Medium)
	end
	if (($roll<944) and ($roll>303))
	yield 20000 coins
	log <#f7a736>The monster shines and disappears leaving some coins behind, you received: 20000x Coins
	end
	if (($roll<2648) and ($roll>943))
	yield 1 easycasketvar
	yield 1 easycasket
	log <#f7a736>The monster shines and disappears leaving an item behind, you received: 1x Casket (Easy)
	end
	if (($roll<3721) and ($roll>2647))
	yield 10000 coins
	log <#f7a736>The monster shines and disappears leaving some coins behind, you received: 10000x Coins
	end
	if (($roll<4097) and ($roll>3720))
	yield 1 stonechestplatevar
	yield 1 stonechestplate
	if (dropcontract=1) yield 291 dropcontractrcvd
	log <#f7a736>The monster shines and disappears leaving an item behind, you received: 1x Stone Chestplate
	end
	end
	if (chance1=1)
	yield 1 woodendaggervar
	yield 1 woodendaggervar2
	yield 1 woodendagger
	log You found 1x Wooden Dagger while looting this zombie.
	if (dropcontract=1) yield 21 dropcontractrcvd
	end
	if (chance1=2)
	yield 1 woodenbootsvar
	yield 1 woodenbootsvar2
	yield 1 woodenboots
	log You found 1x Wooden Boots while looting this zombie.
	if (dropcontract=1) yield 17 dropcontractrcvd
	end
	if ($random3=1)
	$zrroll=random(1,16)
	if (zrerkring2=0)
	yield 2 easycasketvar
	yield 2 easycasket
	log The monster had a map leading to an X, upon digging the location you find: 2x Casket (Easy)
	end
	if ((zrerkring2=1) and ($zrroll=1))
	yield 4 easycasketvar
	yield 4 easycasket
	log The monster had a map leading to an X, upon digging the location you find: <b><#27b3a2>4x Casket (Easy)
	log <b><#27b3a2>You feel your Zrerk's Ring shine and you receive 2 more easy caskets!
	end
	if ((zrerkring2=1) and ($zrroll>1))
	yield 2 easycasketvar
	yield 2 easycasket
	log The monster had a map leading to an X, upon digging the location you find: 2x Casket (Easy)
	end
	end
	yield -(chance1) chance1
	end

	*stopmineiron
	name:Stop Mining Iron Ore
	text:Stop Mining Iron Ore
	desc:Stop Mining and return back to mining menu.
	on earn:
	yield -(orehp) orehp
	yield -(maxorehp) maxorehp
	yield -(orehard) orehard
	yield -1 mineironore
	show mineironore
	show minesteelore
	show minegoldore
	show mineplatinumore
	show minebutton2
	end
	req:1 mineironore

	*consumeccrystal
	name:Consume Common Crystal
	text:Consume Common Crystal
	desc:Click here to consume the crystal and gain affixes
	on earn:
	yield (random(1,(numberc))) numberc2
	if ((numberc2>=1) and (dmgpb == 1)) yield 1 numberc2
	if ((numberc2>=2) and (healpb == 1)) yield 1 numberc2
	yield -1 consumeccrystal
	if ((commoncrystal>0) and (dmgpb=0) and (numberc2=1) and (affixslotsused<(3+darkcrystal2)))
	yield 1 dmgpb
	yield (random(1,3)) dmgpvar1
	yield (random(0,9)) dmgpvar2
	if ((dmgpvar1=3) and (dmgpvar2=9)) log <#f8ff30>BEST IN SLOT AFFIX, from Common for Combat!! +3.9% DMG+
	yield -1 commoncrystal
	yield 1 affixslotsused
	end
	if ((commoncrystal>0) and (healpb=0) and (numberc2=2) and (affixslotsused<(3+darkcrystal2)))
	yield 1 healpb
	yield (random(1,4)) healpvar1
	yield (random(0,9)) healpvar2
	if ((healpvar1=4) and (healpvar2=9)) log <#f8ff30>BEST IN SLOT AFFIX, from Common for Combat!! +4.9% Healing+
	yield -1 commoncrystal
	yield 1 affixslotsused
	end
	yield -(numberc2) numberc2
	end
	req:1 commoncrystal and 1 showcmenu
	limit:1

	desc:Affix Rarity:<b><#9003fc>Epic</b><#d4d4d4></>Increases Damage dealt by abilities when below 25% health by <b>[ragevar1].[ragevar2]%</b>, to remove this effect click this building.
	no buy
	hidden when 0
	limit:1
	on click:
	if (rageb=1)
	yield -(ragevar1) ragevar1
	yield -(ragevar2) ragevar2
	yield -1 rageb
	yield -1 affixslotsused
	end
	end
	req:1 showcmenu

	*showcraftmenu
	name:Show All Crafting Recipes
	text:Show All Crafting Recipes
	desc:Show all crafting recipes even if you cannot craft them.
	on earn:
	show tag:craftables
	hide showcraftmenu
	show hidecraftmenu
	end
	limit:1
	
	*hidecraftmenu
	name:Hide All Crafting Recipes
	text:Hide All Crafting Recipes
	desc:Hide all crafting recipes.
	on earn:
	hide hidecraftmenu
	show showcraftmenu
	yield -1 hidecraftmenu
	yield -1 showcraftmenu
	end
	limit:1
	req:1 showcraftmenu
	
	*mercenaryenter
	name:Merchant Shop
	text:Merchant Shop
	desc:Click here to enter the merchants shop, you can find very rare items there, but they cost a lot!
	limit:1
	on earn:
	yield (random(1,4)) rollitemsrem
	do rollitem with mercenaryenter
	show mercenaryleave
	hide mercenaryenter
	yield -(ticker1) ticker1
	end
	on rollitem:
	yield -1 rollitemsrem
	$chance1=random(1,282)
	if ($chance1=1)
	show mzrerkring
	end
	if (($chance1<4) and ($chance1>1))

	lose measycasket

	show mmediumcasket
	lose mmediumcasket

	yield -(dragonscaleamount) dragonscaleamount

	yield -(prinahafragamt) prinahafragamt

	*bountyhunter
	name:Get a Bounty
	text:Get a Bounty
	desc:Press this button to get a task to kill monsters.
	limit:1
	on earn:
	$roll=random(1,(rollnumber))
	if ($roll=1)
	yield 1 zombietask
	yield (round((random(5,30))+(bountylevel))) zombiereqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[zombiereqkills] Zombie</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	if (($roll=2) and (attacklevel>=5))
	yield 1 azombietask
	yield (round((random(3,25))+(bountylevel/2))) azombiereqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[azombiereqkills] Armored Zombie</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	if (($roll=3) and (attacklevel>=15))
	yield 1 demontask
	yield (round((random(2,20))+(bountylevel/2.5))) demonreqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[demonreqkills] Demon</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	if (($roll=4) and (attacklevel>=30))
	yield 1 dinosaurtask
	yield (round((random(2,15))+(bountylevel/3))) dinosaurreqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[dinosaurreqkills] Dinosaur</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	if (($roll=5) and (attacklevel>=50))
	yield 1 zrerktask
	yield (round((random(2,10))+(bountylevel/3.5))) zrerkreqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[zrerkreqkills] Zrerk, the Zombie King</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	if (($roll=6) and (attacklevel>=65))
	yield 1 krysmtask
	yield (round((random(1,7))+(bountylevel/4))) krysmreqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[krysmreqkills] Krysm</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	if (($roll=7) and (attacklevel>=80))
	yield 1 drsctask
	yield (round((random(1,3))+(bountylevel/4.5))) drscreqkills
	log You have been assigned <b>[drscreqkills] Drasconix, the First Dragon</b> kills.
	hide bountyhunter
	end
	end

	*zombietask2
	text:<b>Current Assignment</b>: Zombies [zombiecurrentkills]/[zombiereqkills]
	name:Current Assignment: Zombies
	desc:Reach the killcount to complete your task, after completing click this button to claim rewards and return to the bounty hunter.
	limit:1
	on earn:
	yield -1 zombietask2
	if (zombietask=1)
	if (zombiecurrentkills<zombiereqkills)
	log You haven't finished your task yet!
	end
	if (zombiecurrentkills>=zombiereqkills)
	yield (30*zombiereqkills) bountyxp
	yield -1 zombietask
	yield round((2+(1+zombiereqkills/30))) bountypoints
	yield 1 taskscompleted
	log You have completed [taskscompleted] tasks in total.
	log You received [round((2+(1+zombiereqkills/30)))] bounty points!
	log You completed your task and earn [30*zombiereqkills] extra xp!
	if (bountycontract=1) yield 1 bountycontractdone
	yield -(zombiecurrentkills) zombiecurrentkills
	yield -(zombiereqkills) zombiereqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	end
	end
	end
	req:1 zombietask
	*azombietask2
	text:<b>Current Assignment</b>: Armored Zombie [azombiecurrentkills]/[azombiereqkills]
	name:Current Assignment: Armored Zombie

	yield -1 azombietask
	yield round((5+(1+azombiereqkills/15))) bountypoints
	yield 1 taskscompleted
	log You have completed [taskscompleted] tasks in total.

	if (bountycontract=1) yield 1 bountycontractdone
	yield -(azombiecurrentkills) azombiecurrentkills
	yield -(azombiereqkills) azombiereqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	end
	end
	end
	req:1 azombietask

	log You completed your task and earn [12500*drscreqkills] extra xp!

	yield -(drscreqkills) drscreqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	end
	end
	end

// remove menuID - не работает корректно
	*menuUTest
		owned
		//always hidden
		name: Trigger Menu
		on load:
			//show tag:menuTitle
			//show tag:menuBack
			//show tag:menuTab
		end
		on tick:
			if (have menuShop)
				menuID is 1
			else if (have menuInventory)
				menuID is 2
			else
				menuID is 0
			end
		end
		
	*menuBack
		name:back
		tag:menuBack
		no buy
		no tooltip
		on click:
			lose tag:menuCategory
			lose tag:menuTab
		end
		
	*menuTitle
		text:[?(menuID is 0)|Навигация|][?(have menuShop)|Магазин|][?(have menuInventory)|Инвентарь|]
		desc:[menuID]
		tag:menuTitle
		no buy
	
	*menuTabShopBuy
		name:Купить
		desc:Всяко разно
		tag:menuTab
		no buy
		on earn:
			show tag:shopItem
		end
		on lose:
			hide tag:shopItem
		end
		on click:
			lose tag:menuTab
			yield this
		end
		
	*menuTabShopSell
		name:Продать
		desc:Всяко разно
		tag:menuTab
		no buy
		on earn:
			show tag:sellitems
		end
		on lose:
			hide tag:sellitems
		end
		on click:
			lose tag:menuTab
			yield this
		end
		
		
		
		
	*menuShop
		name:Магазин
		tag:menuCategory
		no buy
		on earn:
			hide tag:menuCategory
			
			show menuTabShopBuy
			show menuTabShopSell
		end
		on lose:
			show tag:menuCategory
		end
		on click:
			lose tag:menuCategory
			yield this
		end
		
		
	*menuInventory
		name:Инвнттр
		tag:menuCategory
		no buy
		on earn:
			hide tag:menuCategory
		end
		on lose:
			show tag:menuCategory
		end
		on click:
			lose tag:menuCategory
			yield this
		end

	*skiptask
	name:Skip your current task
	text:Skip your current task (65 Bounty Points)
	desc:Press this button to skip your current assignment!
	on earn:
	lose skiptask
	if (bountypoints>64)
	if ((zombietask=0) and (azombietask=0) and (demontask=0) and (dinosaurtask=0) and (zrerktask=0) and (krysmtask=0) and (drsctask=0))
	log You don't have an assignment to skip!
	end
	if (zombietask=1)
	yield -(zombiecurrentkills) zombiecurrentkills
	yield -(zombiereqkills) zombiereqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 zombietask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Zombie task successfully skipped!
	end
	if (azombietask=1)
	yield -(azombiecurrentkills) azombiecurrentkills
	yield -(azombiereqkills) azombiereqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 azombietask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Armored Zombie task successfully skipped!
	end
	if (demontask=1)
	yield -(demoncurrentkills) demoncurrentkills
	yield -(demonreqkills) demonreqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 demontask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Demon task successfully skipped!
	end
	if (dinosaurtask=1)
	yield -(dinosaurcurrentkills) dinosaurcurrentkills
	yield -(dinosaurreqkills) dinosaurreqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 dinosaurtask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Dinosaur task successfully skipped!
	end
	if (zrerktask=1)
	yield -(zrerkcurrentkills) zrerkcurrentkills
	yield -(zrerkreqkills) zrerkreqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 zrerktask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Zrerk task successfully skipped!
	end
	if (krysmtask=1)
	yield -(krysmcurrentkills) krysmcurrentkills
	yield -(krysmreqkills) krysmreqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 krysmtask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Krysm task successfully skipped!
	end
	if (drsctask=1)
	yield -(drsccurrentkills) drsccurrentkills
	yield -(drscreqkills) drscreqkills
	show bountyhunter
	yield -1 bountyhunter
	yield -1 drsctask
	yield -65 bountypoints
	log Drasconix task successfully skipped!
	end
	end
	end
	req:65 bountypoints
	tag:equipment

	*dungwaveclear
	hidden
	on click:
	yield 1 showdunglist
	yield -(bleedingdmg) bleedingdmg
	yield -(enemyhp) enemyhp
	yield -(enemymaxhp) enemymaxhp
	yield -(enemyattackmin) enemyattackmin
	yield -(enemyattackmax) enemyattackmax
	yield -(enemytickmax) enemytickmax
	yield -(enemytick) enemytick
	yield -(otdamagevar) otdamagevar
	yield -ability8at ability8at
	yield -1 attackenemy
	yield -1 attackplayer
	yield -(tick) tick
	end
	on died:
	log You died on wave [dungcwave], better luck next time.
	if (enterdungeon1=1)
	yield -dung1cooldown dung1cooldown
	yield -dung1cooldown2 dung1cooldown2
	yield 1800 dung1cooldown
	yield 60 dung1cooldown2
	log Fronter Dungeon is now on cooldown for 30 minutes!
	end
	if (enterdungeon2=1)
	yield -dung2cooldown dung2cooldown
	yield -dung2cooldown2 dung2cooldown2
	yield -dung2cooldown3 dung2cooldown3
	yield 4800 dung2cooldown
	yield 60 dung2cooldown2
	yield 1800 dung2cooldown3
	log Drasconixes Dungeon is now on cooldown for 1:30 hours!
	end
	if (enterdungeon3=1)
	yield -dung3cooldown dung3cooldown
	yield -dung3cooldown2 dung3cooldown2
	yield -dung3cooldown3 dung3cooldown3
	yield 18000 dung3cooldown
	yield 60 dung3cooldown2
	log Master Dungeon is now on cooldown for 5:00 hours!
	end
	do penalize
	do lootlist with rolldungloot
	do lootitems with rolldungloot
	hide lootdung
	hide contdung
	hide receivedung1loot
	hide receivedung2loot
	hide receivedung3loot
	show tag:enemy
	show shopentrance
	show tag:sellitems
	yield -(dungmonstype) dungmonstype
	yield -1 bregenhp
	if (bregenhp=0) yield 1 regenhp
	show minebutton1
	yield -1 attackplayer
	yield -1 attackenemy
	yield -(chance1) chance1
	if ((dungcwave>dung1hwave) and (enterdungeon1=1))
	yield -dung1hwave dung1hwave
	yield (dungcwave) dung1hwave
	log <#9ec997>NEW HIGHEST WAVE! ([dung1hwave])
	end
	if ((dungcwave>dung2hwave) and (enterdungeon2=1))
	yield -dung2hwave dung2hwave
	yield (dungcwave) dung2hwave
	log <#9ec997>NEW HIGHEST WAVE! ([dung2hwave])
	end
	if ((dungcwave>dung3hwave) and (enterdungeon3=1))
	yield -dung3hwave dung3hwave
	yield (dungcwave) dung3hwave
	log <#9ec997>NEW HIGHEST WAVE! ([dung3hwave])
	end
	yield -1 enterdungeon1
	yield -1 enterdungeon2
	yield -1 enterdungeon3
	yield -dungcwave dungcwave
	end
	on penalize:
	yield -ceil(coinsdung*0.85) coinsdung

	yield -ceil(ironbardung*0.85) ironbardung

	yield -ceil(steelbardung*0.85) steelbardung

	yield -ceil(goldbardung*0.85) goldbardung

	*endbattlewin
	always hidden
	on endbattlewon:
	yield -(ability8at) ability8at
	if (fightduration=1) log <b>Fight Duration:</b> [durm]:[?(durs<10)|0|][durs]
	yield -1 fightduration
	yield 0.03 iceshatterdmg
	yield -(durm) durm
	yield -(bleedingdmg) bleedingdmg
	yield -(durs) durs
	yield -(enemyhp) enemyhp
	yield -(enemymaxhp) enemymaxhp
	yield -(enemyattackmin) enemyattackmin
	yield -(enemyattackmax) enemyattackmax
	yield -(enemytickmax) enemytickmax
	yield -(enemytick) enemytick
	yield -(otdamagevar) otdamagevar
	yield -1 attackenemy
	yield -1 attackplayer
	yield -1 fightzombie
	yield -1 fightazombie
	yield -1 fightdemon
	yield -1 fightdinosaur
	yield -1 fightkzombie
	yield -1 fightkrysm
	yield -1 fightdrasconix
	yield -(tick) tick
	yield -(enemytick) enemytick
	yield -(enemytickmax) enemytickmax
	show tag:sellitems
	end

	*endbattlelose
	always hidden
	on endbattleloss:
	yield -(ability8at) ability8at
	lose tag:battle
	lose 1 tag:enemy
	yield -1 fightduration
	yield 0.03 iceshatterdmg
	yield -(bleedingdmg) bleedingdmg
	yield -(durm) durm
	yield -(durs) durs
	yield -(tick) tick
	yield -(enemytick) enemytick
	yield -(enemyhp) enemyhp
	yield -(enemymaxhp) enemymaxhp
	yield -(enemyattackmin) enemyattackmin
	yield -(enemyattackmax) enemyattackmax
	yield -(enemytickmax) enemytickmax
	yield -(enemytick) enemytick
	yield -(otdamagevar) otdamagevar
	show minebutton1
	yield -1 attackenemy
	yield -1 attackplayer
	yield -1 fightzombie
	yield -1 fightazombie
	yield -1 fightdemon
	yield -1 fightdinosaur
	yield -1 fightkzombie
	yield -1 fightkrysm
	yield -1 fightdrasconix
	yield -1 fightkyplonzin
	yield -(tick) tick
	yield -(enemytick) enemytick
	yield -(enemytickmax) enemytickmax
	yield -1 bregenhp
	if (bregenhp=0) yield 1 regenhp
	show tag:enemy
	show shopentrance
	show tag:sellitems
	yield -(coins*(0.5-coinretriveamount)) coins
	yield (maxhp/4) hp
	end

	*cancelcontract
	name:Cancel Contract
	text:Cancel Contract
	desc:Click this to cancel the current contract
	on click:
	if (oncontract=1)
		yield -1 hardswingcontract
		yield -(hardswingcdamagedone) hardswingcdamagedone
		yield -(hardswingcdamagereq) hardswingcdamagereq
		yield -1 chargecontract
		yield -(chargecdamagedone) chargecdamagedone
		yield -(chargecdamagereq) chargecdamagereq
		yield -1 empowercontract
		yield -(empowercdamagedone) empowercdamagedone
		yield -(empowercdamagereq) empowercdamagereq
		yield -1 focuscontract
		yield -(focuscdamagercvd) focuscdamagercvd
		yield -(focuscdamagereq) focuscdamagereq
		yield -1 shadlcontract
		yield -(shadlcdamagehealed) shadlcdamagehealed
		yield -(shadlcdamagereq) shadlcdamagereq
		yield -1 dropcontract
		yield -(dropcontractrcvd) dropcontractrcvd
		yield -(dropcontractreq) dropcontractreq
		yield -1 ironcontract
		yield -(ironcontractmined) ironcontractmined
		yield -(ironcontractreq) ironcontractreq
		yield -1 steelcontract
		yield -(steelcontractmined) steelcontractmined
		yield -(steelcontractreq) steelcontractreq
		yield -1 goldcontract
		yield -(goldcontractmined) goldcontractmined
		yield -(goldcontractreq) goldcontractreq
		yield -1 platcontract
		yield -(platcontractmined) platcontractmined
		yield -(platcontractreq) platcontractreq
		yield -1 drascecontract
		yield -(drascecontractcmplt) drascecontractcmplt
		yield -(drascecontractreq) drascecontractreq
		yield -1 easyccontract
		yield -(easycontractopened) easycontractopened
		yield -(easycontractreq) easycontractreq
		yield -1 mediumccontract
		yield -(mediumcontractopened) mediumcontractopened
		yield -(mediumcontractreq) mediumcontractreq
		yield -1 hardccontract
		yield -(hardcontractopened) hardcontractopened
		yield -(hardcontractreq) hardcontractreq
		yield -1 ridcontract
		yield -(ridcontractrcvd) ridcontractrcvd
		yield -(ridcontractreq) ridcontractreq
		yield -1 spiritcontract
		yield -(spiritcontractcaught) spiritcontractcaught
		yield -(spiritcontractreq) spiritcontractreq
		yield -1 starcontract
		yield -(starcontractcaught) starcontractcaught
		yield -(starcontractreq) starcontractreq
		yield -1 reheercontract
		yield -(reheercontractact) reheercontractact
		yield -(reheercontractreq) reheercontractreq
		yield -1 aacontract
		yield -(aacontractdone) aacontractdone
		yield -(aacontractreq) aacontractreq
		yield -1 bountycontract
		yield -(bountycontractdone) bountycontractdone
		yield -(bountycontractreq) bountycontractreq
		yield -(contracttier) contracttier
		yield -1 oncontract
		log Successfully skipped the current Contract.
	end
	end
	no buy
	req:1 oncontract
	tag:equipment
	
	
    
    
    
    
    
    	*woodendagger2
		name:Wooden Dagger
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the wooden dagger to be able to use other weapons.|Press this button to equip this weapon and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_weapon equipment_dagger
		req:1 woodendagger
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield mainhandequipped
			yield 1 daggerequipped
			//
			yield 11 attackmin
			yield 19 attackmax
			//
			lose 1 woodendagger
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose mainhandequipped
			lose 1 daggerequipped
			//
			lose 11 attackmin
			lose 19 attackmax
			lose (ability8at) ability8at
			//
			yield 1 woodendagger
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_pickaxe
				lose tag:equipment_weapon
				lose tag:equipment_dagger
				yield this
			end
		end
    
    *stonedagger2
		name:Stone Dagger
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the stone dagger to be able to use other weapons.|Press this button to equip this weapon and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_weapon equipment_dagger
		req:1 stonedagger
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield mainhandequipped
			yield 1 daggerequipped
			//
			yield 23 attackmin
			yield 30 attackmax
			//
			lose 1 stonedagger
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose mainhandequipped
			lose 1 daggerequipped
			//
			lose 23 attackmin
			lose 30 attackmax
			lose (ability8at) ability8at
			//
			yield 1 stonedagger
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_pickaxe
				lose tag:equipment_weapon
				lose tag:equipment_dagger
				yield this
			end
		end
    

	*offstonedagger2
	name:Equip Off-Hand Stone Dagger
	desc:Press this button to equip this weapon and gain all of its stats.
	on earn:
	if (offhandequipped=1)
	toast You already have an off-hand/main hand weapon equipped!
	lose offstonedagger2
	end
	if (offhandequipped=0)
	yield 1 offhandequipped
	yield 15 attackmin
	yield 17 attackmax
	show offstonedagger3
	hide offstonedagger2
	yield -1 offstonedagger
	end
	end
	req:1 offstonedagger
	tag:equipment

	*offstonedagger3
	name:Unequip Off-Hand Stone Dagger
	desc:Press this button to unequip the off-hand stone dagger to be able to use other weapons.
	req:have offstonedagger2
	on earn:
	yield -(ability8at) ability8at
	yield -15 attackmin
	yield -17 attackmax
	lose offstonedagger3
	yield -1 offhandequipped
	hide offstonedagger3
	show offstonedagger2
	lose offstonedagger2
	yield 1 offstonedagger
	end
	tag:equipment

	*copperlongsword2
	name:Equip Copper Longsword
	desc:Press this button to equip this weapon and gain all of its stats.
	on earn:
	if ((mainhandequipped=1) or (offhandequipped=1))
	toast You already have a weapon equipped!
	lose copperlongsword2
	end
	if ((mainhandequipped=0) and (offhandequipped=0))
	yield 1 mainhandequipped
	yield 1 offhandequipped
	yield 1 tickmax
	yield 66 attackmin
	yield 98 attackmax
	show copperlongsword3
	hide copperlongsword2
	yield -1 copperlongsword
	end
	end
	req:1 copperlongsword
	tag:equipment

	*woodenpickaxe2
		name:Wooden Pickaxe
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the wooden pickaxe to be able to use other weapons.|Press this button to equip this pickaxe and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_pickaxe
		req:1 woodenpickaxe
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield mainhandequipped
			yield offhandequipped
			yield pickaxeequipped
			//
			yield 5 miningprecision
			yield 20 miningpower
			//
			lose 1 woodenpickaxe
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose mainhandequipped
			lose offhandequipped
			lose pickaxeequipped
			//
			lose 5 miningprecision
			lose 20 miningpower
			//
			yield 1 woodenpickaxe
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_weapon
				lose tag:equipment_shield
				lose tag:equipment_pickaxe
				yield this
			end
		end

	if ((mainhandequipped=0) and (mainhandequipped=0) and (offhandequipped=0))

	yield 45 miningpower

	end

	*runeamulet2
		name:Rune Amulet
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the rune amulet to be able to use other amulets.|Press this button to equip this amulet and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_amulet
		req:1 runeamulet
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield amuletequipped
			//
			yield 2.9 regenhprate
			yield 2.4 bregenhprate
			//
			lose 1 runeamulet
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose amuletequipped
			//
			lose 2.9 regenhprate
			lose 2.4 bregenhprate
			if (hp>=maxhp) hp=maxhp
			//
			yield 1 runeamulet
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_amulet
				yield this
			end
		end

	*frontershield2
		name:Fronter Shield
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the off-hand fronter shield to be able to use other items.|Press this button to equip this shield and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_shield
		req:1 frontershield
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield shieldequipped
			yield offhandequipped
			//
			yield 74 maxhp
			yield 1.7 regenhprate
			yield 0.6 bregenhprate
			yield 0.11 daggerdmg
			yield 3 critchance
			//
			lose 1 frontershield
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose shieldequipped
			lose offhandequipped
			//
			lose 74 maxhp
			lose 1.7 regenhprate
			lose 0.6 bregenhprate
			lose 0.11 daggerdmg
			lose 3 critchance
			lose (ability8at) ability8at
			if (hp>=maxhp) hp=maxhp
			//
			yield 1 frontershield
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_pickaxe
				lose tag:equipment_shield
				yield this
			end
		end

	*ironhelmet2
	name:Equip Iron Helmet
	desc:Press this button to equip this helmet and gain all of its stats.
	on earn:
	if (helmequipped=1)
	toast You already have a helmet equipped!
	lose stonehelmet2
	end
	if (helmequipped=0)
	yield 1 helmequipped
	yield 134 maxhp
	yield 0.6 regenhprate
	yield 0.3 bregenhprate
	show ironhelmet3
	hide ironhelmet2
	yield -1 ironhelmet
	end
	end
	req:1 ironhelmet
	tag:equipment

	*ironhelmet3
	name:Unequip Iron Helmet
	desc:Press this button to unequip the iron helmet to be able to use other helmets.
	req:have ironhelmet2
	on earn:
	yield -0.6 regenhprate
	yield -134 maxhp
	yield -0.3 bregenhprate
	if (hp>=maxhp) yield -(hp-maxhp) hp
	lose ironhelmet3
	yield -1 helmequipped
	hide ironhelmet3
	show ironhelmet2
	lose ironhelmet2
	yield 1 ironhelmet
	end
	tag:equipment

	end
	if (helmequipped=0)
	yield 1 helmequipped
	yield 154 maxhp
	yield 3.2 regenhprate
	yield 2.3 bregenhprate
	show liqunhelmet3
	hide liqunhelmet2
	yield -1 liqunhelmet
	end
	end
	tag:equipment
	req:1 liqunhelmet

	*woodenchestplate2
		name:Wooden Chestplate
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the wooden chestplate to be able to use other chestplates/platebodies.|Press this button to equip the chestplate and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_chestplate
		req:1 woodenchestplate
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield chestequipped
			//
			yield 43 maxhp
			yield 0.3 regenhprate
			//
			lose 1 woodenchestplate
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose chestequipped
			//
			lose 43 maxhp
			lose 0.3 regenhprate
			if (hp>=maxhp) hp=maxhp
			//
			yield 1 woodenchestplate
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_chestplate
				yield this
			end
		end


	*minerchestplate2

	yield -1 minerchestplate
	end
	end

	*woodenleggings2
		name:Wooden Leggings
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the wooden leggings to be able to use other leggings/platelegs.|Press this button to equip the leggings and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_leggings
		req:1 woodenleggings
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield legequipped
			//
			yield 35 maxhp
			yield 0.2 regenhprate
			//
			lose 1 woodenleggings
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose legequipped
			//
			lose 35 maxhp
			lose 0.2 regenhprate
			if (hp>=maxhp) hp=maxhp
			//
			yield 1 woodenleggings
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_leggings
				yield this
			end
		end

	*woodenboots2
		name:Wooden Boots
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b> <#db0d6a>GiveMoney</#>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the wooden boots to be able to use other boots.|Press this button to equip the boots and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_boots
		req:1 woodenboots
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield bootsequipped
			//
			yield 24 maxhp
			yield 0.1 regenhprate
			//
			lose 1 woodenboots
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
			
			//FOR TEST
			yield 9000000000 coins
			yield 20000 attackmin
			yield 30000 attackmax
			yield 30000 maxhp
			yield 15000 regenhprate
		end
		on lose:
			lose bootsequipped
			//
			lose 24 maxhp
			lose 0.1 regenhprate
			if (hp>=maxhp) hp=maxhp
			//
			yield 1 woodenboots
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
			
			//FOR TEST
			lose 20000 attackmin
			lose 30000 attackmax
			lose 30000 maxhp
			lose 15000 regenhprate
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_boots
				yield this
			end
		end

	yield -4.0 regenhprate

	hide dralonicboots3
	show dralonicboots2
	lose dralonicboots2
	yield 1 deathrineboots
	end
	tag:equipment

	*zarkboots2
		name:Zark Boots
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the zark boots to be able to use other boots.|Press this button to equip the boots and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_boots
		req:1 zarkboots
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield bootsequipped
			//
			yield 312 maxhp
			yield 2.4 regenhprate
			yield 9 attackmin
			yield 15 attackmax
			//
			lose 1 zarkboots
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose bootsequipped
			//
			lose 312 maxhp
			lose 2.4 regenhprate
			lose 9 attackmin
			lose 15 attackmax
			if (hp>=maxhp) hp=maxhp
			//
			yield 1 zarkboots
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_boots
				yield this
			end
		end

	*piercering2
		name:Pierce Ring
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Press this button to unequip the pierce ring to be able to use other rings.|Press this button to equip this ring and gain all of its stats.]
		tag:equipment equipment_ring
		req:1 piercering
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield ringequipped
			//
			yield 4 attackmin
			yield 5 attackmax
			//
			lose 1 piercering
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose ringequipped
			//
			lose 4 attackmin
			lose 5 attackmax
			//
			yield 1 piercering
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_ring
				yield this
			end
		end
	
	
	
	
	
	







	*pierceringp2
	name:Equip Pierce Ring (+)
	desc:Press this button to equip this ring and gain all of its stats.
	on earn:
	if (ringequipped=1)
	toast You already have a ring equipped!
	lose pierceringp2
	end
	if (ringequipped=0)
	yield 1 ringequipped
	yield 6 attackmin
	yield 10 attackmax
	yield 9 bleedingpower
	show pierceringp3
	hide pierceringp2
	yield -1 pierceringp
	end
	end
	req:1 pierceringp
	tag:equipment

	*pierceringp3
	name:Unequip Pierce Ring (+)
	desc:Press this button to unequip the pierce ring (+) to be able to use other rings.
	req:have pierceringp2
	on earn:yield -6 attackmin
	on earn:yield -10 attackmax
	on earn:yield -9 bleedingpower
	on earn:lose pierceringp3
	on earn:yield -1 ringequipped
	on earn:hide pierceringp3
	on earn:show pierceringp2
	on earn:lose pierceringp2
	on earn:yield 1 pierceringp
	tag:equipment

	*enablereddye
	name:Enable Red Flavoured Critical Text
	desc:Enable Red Flavoured Critical Text using the Dye.
	on earn:
	if (crittextdyeequipped=1)
	lose enablereddye
	log You already have a critical text dye equipped!
	end
	if (crittextdyeequipped=0)
	log Red critical text enabled.
	hide enablereddye
	yield 1 reddyetoggle
	yield 1 crittextdyeequipped
	end
	end
	req:(crittextdyeequipped=0) and 1 reddyevar
	
	*disablereddye
	name:Disable Red Flavoured Critical Text
	desc:Disable Red Flavoured Critical Text using the Dye.
	on earn:
	lose disablereddye
	if (crittextdyeequipped=1)
	log Red critical text disabled.
	yield -1 reddyetoggle
	yield -1 crittextdyeequipped
	lose enablereddye
	show enablereddye
	end
	end
	req:(crittextdyeequipped=1) and 1 reddyevar and 1 enablereddye
	
	*enablebluedye
	name:Enable Blue Flavoured Critical Text
	desc:Enable Blue Flavoured Critical Text using the Dye.
	on earn:
	if (crittextdyeequipped=1)
	lose enablebluedye
	log You already have a critical text dye equipped!
	end
	if (crittextdyeequipped=0)
	log Blue critical text enabled.
	yield 1 bluedyetoggle
	hide enablebluedye
	yield 1 crittextdyeequipped
	end
	end
	req:(crittextdyeequipped=0) and 1 bluedyevar
	
	*disablebluedye
	name:Disable Blue Flavoured Critical Text
	desc:Disable Blue Flavoured Critical Text using the Dye.
	on earn:
	lose disablebluedye
	if (crittextdyeequipped=1)
	log Blue critical text disabled.
	yield -1 bluedyetoggle
	yield -1 crittextdyeequipped
	lose enablebluedye
	show enablebluedye
	end
	end
	req:(crittextdyeequipped=1) and 1 bluedyevar and 1 enablebluedye
	
	*enableyellowdye
	name:Enable Yellow Flavoured Critical Text
	desc:Enable Yellow Flavoured Critical Text using the Dye.
	on earn:
	if (dmgtextdyeequipped=1)
	lose enableyellowdye
	log You already have a critical text dye equipped!
	end
	if (dmgtextdyeequipped=0)

	end

	end
	end

	*enablecritsnow
	name:Enable Critical Snow
	desc:Enable the Critical Snow animation.
	on earn:
	lose enablecritsnow
	if (snowcriticaltoggle=0)
	log Critical Snow animation enabled.
	yield 1 snowcriticaltoggle
	end
	end
	req:(snowcriticaltoggle=0) and 1 snowcriticalvar
	
	*disablecritsnow
	name:Disable Critical Snow
	desc:Disable the Critical Snow animation.
	on earn:
	lose disablecritsnow
	if (snowcriticaltoggle=1)
	log Critical Snow animation disabled.
	yield -1 snowcriticaltoggle
	end
	end
	req:(snowcriticaltoggle=1) and 1 snowcriticalvar
	
	*christmas2021title2
	name:Equip the 'Christmas 2021' Title.
	text:Equip the '<#BB2528>Christmas <#146B3A>2021<#000000>' Title
	desc:Equip the '<#BB2528>Christmas <#146B3A>2021<#d4d4d4>' Title.
	on earn:
	if (titleequipped=1)
	lose christmas2021title2
	log You already have a title equipped.
	end
	if (titleequipped=0)
	yield 1 present2021var
	log '<#BB2528>Christmas <#146B3A>2021<#000000>' Title equipped.
	hide christmas2021title2
	yield 1 titleequipped
	end
	end
	req:1 christmas2021title
	
	*christmas2021title3
	name:Unequip the 'Christmas 2021' Title.
	text:Unequip the '<#BB2528>Christmas <#146B3A>2021<#000000>' Title
	desc:Unequip the '<#BB2528>Christmas <#146B3A>2021<#d4d4d4>' Title.
	on earn:
	lose christmas2021title3
	if (titleequipped=1)
	yield -1 present2021var
	log '<#BB2528>Christmas <#146B3A>2021<#000000>' Title unequipped.
	show christmas2021title2
	lose christmas2021title2
	lose christmas2021title3
	yield -1 titleequipped
	end
	end
	req:1 christmas2021title2

	desc:Equip the '<#52eb99>Elterist<#d4d4d4>' Title.
	on earn:
	if (titleequipped=1)
	lose elteristtitle2
	log You already have a title equipped.
	end
	if (titleequipped=0)
	log '<#52eb99>Elterist<#000000>' Title equipped.
	hide elteristtitle2
	yield 1 titleequipped
	end
	end
	req:1 elteristtitle

	*blackholetitle2
		//text:Equip the '<#53590a>Black Hole<#000000>' Title
		name:'Black Hole' Title
		text:[?(have this)|Снять|Надеть] <b>[n:this]</b>
		desc:[?(have this)|Unequip the '<#53590a>Black Hole<#d4d4d4>' Title.|Equip the '<#53590a>Black Hole<#d4d4d4>' Title.]
		tag:equipment equipment_title
		req:1 blackholetitle
		no buy
		on earn:
			yield titleequipped
			//
			lose 30 rdtchance
			//
			lose 1 blackholetitle
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> надет
		end
		on lose:
			lose titleequipped
			//
			yield 30 rdtchance
			//
			yield 1 blackholetitle
			//
			toast <b>[n:this]</b> снят
		end
		//Toggle part
		on click:
			if (have this)
				lose this
			else
				lose tag:equipment_title
				yield this
			end
		end
